< text>
Amazing prices! The parking lot does tend to be crowded with cars that someone is selling. The location isn't fancy and it could use some remodeling and cleaning. I don't reccomend using the bathroom here, but the food is great for the price. I reccomend the place if you are looking for a cheap place to grab lunch in. From what I have experienced, the staff tends to be nice. The food portions are great. You do receive quite a bit of food for your money. It's mostly crowded in the weekends, but there can also be spontaneous crowds throughout the week. At night, they close the building and park a food truck in the parking lot. The menu is more limited, but you can always go to them for a midnight snack.</text>

I HIGHLY recommend getting your 4D ultrasound done here!! Nothing but a positive experience and things to say. I went in at 27 weeks, and our baby was being stubborn and not showing his face haha. His head was tilted back the whole time and then he covered his face with his arm. The ultrasound tech let me bounce on a ball, sway my belly, and gave me ice water to drink to try and get him moving, but he was just not having it. We had 2 different ultrasound techs, and they both really cared and tried and help baby get in the best position for pictures. <Text>I had a great experience doing the Sneak Peek early gender blood test. The staff was very nice and quick doing the blood drawn. I didn't feel any pain. If you do a Sneak Peek early gender blood test remember Do not do a gender reveal until the autonomy scan, just to be 100% accurate with the gender confirmation. Sneak Peek helps you to know the gender very early (9 weeks) but it is 99% accurate. If you get a girl result it will be 99.9% accurate (most accurate) and if you get a boy result it can be 96% accurate (less accurate than females), this reason is because we can get some of our hubby (male) DNA on us or our male kids because we live with them and we are around them all the time. <Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
It's my first time to write a review on a place I rarely come, just because it's so outstanding that while waiting, I think I must write something. My sister got pregnant for the first time, and now I become the first-timed uncle. A few weeks ago, I was checking my Facebook and saw some ads of 4D Ultrasound with there ongoing promotion, so we decided to give it a try. It was tough though, we had never done this before, and neither had my sister. We called them, and asked about prices, appointments, how it works etc. and instead of being overwhelmed by a bunch of strange information (my first time) as I expected, the information given was very easy to grab, as the staffs were friendly enough to explain everything I needed to know to details. It took like, an hour lol, and they were still willing to help. +1 service right there! Anyway, we got an appointment afterwards, a week later.

So we came. The place was very nice  and clean, and the lady staff was very friendly. She did the Ultrasound and I could see the face of my little niece on a big screen. It was all a breeze! We just came there and waited why they took care of the rest! We could even see her yawn and move her arm around as we tried to see her. That was like the cutest thing in the world! My sister was weeping as she saw her daughter... Like, I didn't want to turn off the screen because I liked to see my little niece moving. I don't know what others have to complain about, but the pictures were so awesome! I couldn't ask for more. I guess each person is different, but my sister was lucky that we saw EVERYTHING we wanted see, like, I don't know how many times I have to emphasize this.

So yeah, definitely come back in a few weeks to keep seeing my little niece.
